                    <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="295">
                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="296">
                      Built by our nephew, Kevin's Cabin is rustic Alaska on the inside and practical steel on the outside. Situated 30 miles east of Fairbanks in a quiet neighborhood where the sled dogs out number the human population! You will not see any city lights here so the Aurora shimmers bright.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="297">
                      The Kevin's Cabin Kitchen is fully equipped with dishes, pots, pans and utensils, small fridge, propane cook stove, microwave, coffee maker, and toaster. Also set up with spices, cooking oil, coffee and tea. A queen and twin bed are located upstairs. The cabin is located 1 mile from the main road and on the edge of a vast wilderness thus very quiet and perfect for viewing the northern lights. If you plan your visit between October and March, bring a parka and winter boots; it can get cold here - still. Paw Print Bed n Sled is home to 20 or so Alaskan huskies. These are authentic racing huskies who have traveled many miles over Alaska's great trails. Some have finished the Iditarod, some are preparing to run it. After their evening meal you will hear the howl of the huskies, celebrating the end of another great Alaskan day.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="298">
                      Located in Pleasant Valley (aka Two Rivers) we are just 3 miles from Chena River Recreational Area where you can fish, canoe, or hike in summer and ski or snowshoe in winter. Another 26 miles down the road is Chena Hotsprings, a unique Alaskan institution! Do not be confused by hotels listed on Expedia, trivago, or other online sites - they are NOT a few miles from Chena Hotsprings - more like 60 miles. In fact, Kevin's Cabin is probably the closest place to the Hotsprings, much more affordable, and with no city lights to compete with the Aurora. We offer a one hour Sleddog ride for $90 or a half day learn to mush adventure for $250.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__seo-reviews" data-reactid="299">
                      <li data-reactid="300"><p data-reactid="301">Kevin cabin is the best place to get unplugged and reconnect back to nature. A unique expereince that no running water nor toilet is in the house. Portable water usage will teach you how to be frugal on resources! At night, the howling of the huskies is something you won't get to hear elsewhere. Judy was really helpful when I didn't managed to get a rental car. The location was right in between Chena hot springs which makes the drive easier when heading back after relaxation! Ohh! There is a chance of seeing the Northern lights too!</p><span data-reactid="302">Calvin</span><span data-reactid="303">2016-10-22T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                      <li data-reactid="304"><p data-reactid="305">Staying at Kevin's Cabin was a real treat! We wanted to stay in a rural location to see the night sky and northern lights better and Kevin's cabin was the perfect one. The hot tub was what really got me excited to book this cabin and Judy said she could be flexible with us using it late at night if we wanted to look for the northern lights. She was quick to respond to any questions we had, and we enjoyed chatting with her and meeting all her wonderful dogs. We also opted for a dog sledding experience through a winter wonderland in the woods around their house. This was a unique experience and we rode around the wilderness for about 30 mins enjoying the scenery and the dogs. The dogs were awesome--some Iditarod champions and others yearlings that are training for it--and it was cool to see them pulling us on the ATV (not enough snow yet for the sled). Judy told us all about the dog mushing world and what it was like to train for the Iditarod. We loved watching her feed the dogs, their howling and eagerness for affection is a must-experience for any resident Alaskan or visitor. The cabin itself was cute and rustic, with a lot of thoughtful touches to it. The lofted bed was very comfortable with warm quilts and covers and we felt nice and toasty at night. The cabin was always cozy as the heater worked great. There were many light fixtures and outlets available which we appreciated given the long dark hours. Judy left all kinds of thoughtful additions in the cabin to make it homey--military-quality parkas, slippers for our feet, flashlights, lots of boardgames and books, plenty of dishes for cooking. The breakfast options included farm fresh eggs from their local chickens, pancake mix and bagels with cream cheese. We ate well each morning. There is no running water and we learned to be frugal with our water usage. The outhouse was very clean, and given that it was winter, we had to mentally be prepared when it was -10 at times at night! But it really was the true Alaskan experience and we appreciated it--and the mainhouse is only a few steps away to use the bathroom and shower. (Judy did say they were thinking of adding a few things to the house such as carpeting and an attached bathroom eventually). The location was special as we were right down the road from Chena hot springs and it was a nice rural getaway as it was about 25 mins from Fairbanks. We loved our stay overall and sadly though we didn't see any Northern Lights we would easily come back again! This was a very cool Alaskan experience and beats any hotel stay.</p><span data-reactid="306">Vanitha</span><span data-reactid="307">2016-11-21T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                      <li data-reactid="308"><p data-reactid="309">This was a really wonderful experience! The little cabin has a beautiful and interesting wooden interior, and is tucked around a corner from the main house so it feels really private. When we arrived Judy showed us around the cabin and made sure we felt comfortable. She had left out fresh flowers on the table, tea and coffee (and coffee machine), plenty of drinking water and food for breakfast. The attention to detail made the stay an absolute delight. The bathroom facilities are a lovely clean, domestic-feeling drop toilet outside the cabin and the shower is in the main house, but both of these were so accessible they didn't feel like much of an inconvenience at all. There is wifi close to the main house, and Judy was very welcoming about us using it whenever we needed. There is also a little store about 2 minutes down the road from the house, so even though you're out of town, you can pick up most necessities or comforts very easily. Overall, this was a wonderful place to stay and if I'm back in the area again, I wouldn't think twice about returning.</p><span data-reactid="310">Jessica</span><span data-reactid="311">2016-06-27T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                      <li data-reactid="312"><p data-reactid="313">We stayed at Kevin's cabin for 3 nights for our honeymoon. We got to see the northern lights right from the outside the cabin. The property is perfectly located away from all the city's light pollution and an easy 30-40 min drive to city and China springs resort. The cabin is clean, really nicely decorated and very comfortable. There is an outhouse for bathroom use which may be inconvenient for some but for us it was a true Alaskan experience. You can use the bathroom and shower in the house that is located on the property 20 steps away from cabin. The dogs howling in the morning was also surprisingly very soothing. The best part about our stay here were the hosts. Judie and her husband are wonderful hosts, they were very responsive and attentive with booking and checking in. Judie would update us via text on the weather, road conditions, traffic, aurora forecast. They had bagels and eggs in the cabin. Extra towels if you want to visit the hot springs, wood if you wanna build fire. They were super accommodating and hospitable. It was a incredibly convinient stay and we'll be staying here again. </p><span data-reactid="314">Wajiha</span><span data-reactid="315">2016-10-31T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="2073">
                      Our home is located in North Pole, AK. We are out of the city lights and under the Northern Lights. A short walk away from Chena Lake you will enjoy all of the recreational year round activities. See the Aurora overhead right outside our front door in the winter or enjoy the land of the Midnight Sun in Summer! Our home is located in a quiet location and has all the amenities for your stay here in Alaska. Kayaks, canoe, rafts, ATV, bicycles, snow machines and fishing gear available.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2074">
                      Our home is 10 miles from Fairbanks away from the city lights and under the Northern lights. We are next to the lake where you can enjoy all water activities in the summer and great fishing! In the winter time you can enjoy dog mushing, snow machine riding, skiing, walking trails and ice fishing! We have all of the outdoor equipment and tours are also available. After a long day out on the lake, come home to cook up the catch of the day in the fully equipped kitchen - stocked with all the gadgets needed to create your culinary masterpiece. Spend your evenings gathered around the cozy wood-burning stove before retiring to one of the bedrooms to rest up for the next day of Alaskan adventures. Don’t forget to peek out the windows after nightfall, as you might catch a glimpse of the majestic Aurora Borealis dancing above your head! Coming in May 2017, our home will be expanded with an additional full bathroom, recreation room and will be able to occupy 10-12 guests for our larger groups and families. Please message for more info on summer bookings!
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="2075">
                      Perhaps the best feature of this property is its phenomenal location. Sitting next to the lake the lights shine brightly. Nestled away, you’ll have unparalleled access to the recreational lake walking distance from the house, filled with rainbow trout, King salmon, dolly vardon and grayling to satisfy all your fishing needs. It’s no surprise that Alaska is an outdoor enthusiast’s paradise, and this home is ideally situated to enjoy the area’s best hiking and sightseeing! From here, you will be 61 miles from Chena Hot Springs Resort where you can soak your troubles away in the famous natural outdoor pools. 5 minutes away you can sample homemade fudge and sip espresso at The Santa Claus House in the small Alaskan town of North Pole - a family friendly destination guaranteed to bring a smile to everyone’s face! 15 miles up the highway will bring you to the famous Knotty Shop ice cream parlour, known for it’s enticing flavors and quirky gift shop. Regardless of whether you choose to spend your vacation sight seeing, enjoying water activities, snow machine riding through the Alaskan wilderness, this beautiful home is guaranteed to provide the ultimate Alaska stay.

Overall, we had an excellent time here and would stay again and recommend to friends.
